human_fallen_empires_effect_blackjack_take_cards_in_place = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				which = take_place_12
				value = 1
			}
		}
		# добавить перебор
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = ace_of_spades
						value = 1
					}
					not = {
						check_variable = {
							which = ace_of_spades_in_place
							value = 1
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							which = take_place_1
							value = 0
						}
					}
					set_variable = {
						which = take_place_1
						value = 1
					}
					set_variable = {
						which = ace_of_spades_in_place
						value = 1
					}
					set_variable = {
						which = ace_of_spades_in_place_1
						value = 1
					}
					else = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = {
									which = take_place_2
									value = 0
								}
							}
							set_variable = {
								which = take_place_2
								value = 1
							}
							set_variable = {
								which = ace_of_spades_in_place
								value = 1
							}
							set_variable = {
								which = ace_of_spades_in_place_2
								value = 1
							}
							else = {
								if = {
									limit = {
										check_variable = {
											which = take_place_3
											value = 0
										}
									}
									set_variable = {
										which = take_place_3
										value = 1
									}
									set_variable = {
										which = ace_of_spades_in_place
										value = 1
									}
									set_variable = {
										which = ace_of_spades_in_place_3
										value = 1
									}
									else = {
										if = {
											limit = {
												check_variable = {
													which = take_place_4
													value = 0
												}
											}
											set_variable = {
												which = take_place_4
												value = 1
											}
											set_variable = {
												which = ace_of_spades_in_place
												value = 1
											}
											set_variable = {
												which = ace_of_spades_in_place_4
												value = 1
											}
											else = {
												if = {
													limit = {
														check_variable = {
															which = take_place_5
															value = 0

human_fallen_empires_effect_blackjack_turn_0 = {
	event_target:human_fallen_empires_blackjack_target_0 = {
		human_fallen_empires_effect_blackjack_get_card = yes
		human_fallen_empires_effect_blackjack_get_card = yes
		human_fallen_empires_effect_blackjack_calc_cards = yes
		human_fallen_empires_effect_blackjack_take_cards_in_place = yes
		# if = {
		# limit = {
		# check_variable = {
		# which = blackjack_calc
		# value = 21
		# }
		# }
		# set_country_flag = human_fallen_empires_blackjack_turn_0_21
		# }
	}
	event_target:human_fallen_empires_blackjack_target_1 = {
		save_event_target_as = human_fallen_empires_blackjack_target_enemy		
		human_fallen_empires_effect_blackjack_get_card = yes
		human_fallen_empires_effect_blackjack_get_card = yes
		human_fallen_empires_effect_blackjack_calc_cards = yes
		human_fallen_empires_effect_blackjack_take_cards_in_place = yes
		# if = {
		# limit = {
		# check_variable = {
		# which = blackjack_calc
		# value = 21
		# }
		# }
		# set_country_flag = human_fallen_empires_blackjack_turn_0_21
		# }
	}
	event_target:human_fallen_empires_blackjack_target_0 = {
		country_event = {
			id = human_fallen_empires_pirate.150
		}
	}
}

human_fallen_empires_effect_blackjack_next_turn = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			event_target:human_fallen_empires_blackjack_target_0 = {
				has_country_flag = human_fallen_empires_blackjack_end_shown
			}
			event_target:human_fallen_empires_blackjack_target_1 = {
				has_country_flag = human_fallen_empires_blackjack_end_shown
			}
		}
		event_target:human_fallen_empires_blackjack_target_1 = {
			human_fallen_empires_effect_blackjack_clean_all = yes
		}
		event_target:human_fallen_empires_blackjack_target_0 = {
			human_fallen_empires_effect_blackjack_clean_all = yes
			country_event = {
				id = human_fallen_empires_pirate.101
			}
		}
		else = {
			save_event_target_as = human_fallen_empires_blackjack_target_enemy
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_country = event_target:human_fallen_empires_blackjack_target_0
				}
				event_target:human_fallen_empires_blackjack_target_1 = {
					country_event = {
						id = human_fallen_empires_pirate.150
					}
				}
				else = {
					event_target:human_fallen_empires_blackjack_target_0 = {
						country_event = {
							id = human_fallen_empires_pirate.150
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

human_fallen_empires_effect_blackjack_calc_winner = {
	event_target:human_fallen_empires_blackjack_target_0 = {
		set_country_flag = human_fallen_empires_blackjack_end
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = blackjack_calc
					value > 21
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = human_fallen_empires_blackjack_end_bust
		}
		event_target:human_fallen_empires_blackjack_target_1 = {
			set_country_flag = human_fallen_empires_blackjack_end
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = blackjack_calc
						value > 21
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = human_fallen_empires_blackjack_end_bust
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					or = {
						and = {
							event_target:human_fallen_empires_blackjack_target_0 = {
								has_country_flag = human_fallen_empires_blackjack_end_bust
							}
							has_country_flag = human_fallen_empires_blackjack_end_bust
						}
						check_variable = {
							which = blackjack_calc
							value = prev
						}
					}
				}
				# никто не выиграл
				set_country_flag = human_fallen_empires_blackjack_end_stay
				event_target:human_fallen_empires_blackjack_target_0 = {
					set_country_flag = human_fallen_empires_blackjack_end_stay
				}
				else = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							not = {
								event_target:human_fallen_empires_blackjack_target_0 = {
									has_country_flag = human_fallen_empires_blackjack_end_bust
								}
							}
							or = {
								has_country_flag = human_fallen_empires_blackjack_end_bust
								check_variable = {
									which = blackjack_calc
									value < prev
								}
							}
						}
						# выиграл 0
						event_target:human_fallen_empires_blackjack_target_0 = {
							set_country_flag = human_fallen_empires_blackjack_end_win
						}
						else = {
							# выиграл 1
							set_country_flag = human_fallen_empires_blackjack_end_win
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

human_fallen_empires_effect_blackjack_remove_bet = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = human_fallen_empires_blackjack_bet_0
		}
		event_target:human_fallen_empires_blackjack_target_0 = {
			add_energy = @human_fallen_empires_blackjack_bet_0_minus
		}
		event_target:human_fallen_empires_blackjack_target_1 = {
			add_energy = @human_fallen_empires_blackjack_bet_0_minus
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = human_fallen_empires_blackjack_bet_1
		}
		event_target:human_fallen_empires_blackjack_target_0 = {
			add_energy = @human_fallen_empires_blackjack_bet_1_minus
		}
		event_target:human_fallen_empires_blackjack_target_1 = {
			add_energy = @human_fallen_empires_blackjack_bet_1_minus
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = human_fallen_empires_blackjack_bet_2
		}
		event_target:human_fallen_empires_blackjack_target_0 = {
			add_energy = @human_fallen_empires_blackjack_bet_2_minus
		}
		event_target:human_fallen_empires_blackjack_target_1 = {
			add_energy = @human_fallen_empires_blackjack_bet_2_minus
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = human_fallen_empires_blackjack_bet_3
		}
		event_target:human_fallen_empires_blackjack_target_0 = {
			add_energy = @human_fallen_empires_blackjack_bet_3_minus
		}
		event_target:human_fallen_empires_blackjack_target_1 = {
			add_energy = @human_fallen_empires_blackjack_bet_3_minus
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = human_fallen_empires_blackjack_bet_4
		}
		event_target:human_fallen_empires_blackjack_target_0 = {
			add_energy = @human_fallen_empires_blackjack_bet_4_minus
		}
		event_target:human_fallen_empires_blackjack_target_1 = {
			add_energy = @human_fallen_empires_blackjack_bet_4_minus
		}
	}
}

human_fallen_empires_effect_blackjack_calc_bet = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = human_fallen_empires_blackjack_end_win
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = human_fallen_empires_blackjack_bet_0
			}
			add_energy = @human_fallen_empires_blackjack_bet_0
			add_energy = @human_fallen_empires_blackjack_bet_0
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = human_fallen_empires_blackjack_bet_1
			}
			add_energy = @human_fallen_empires_blackjack_bet_1
			add_energy = @human_fallen_empires_blackjack_bet_1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = human_fallen_empires_blackjack_bet_2
			}
			add_energy = @human_fallen_empires_blackjack_bet_2
			add_energy = @human_fallen_empires_blackjack_bet_2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = human_fallen_empires_blackjack_bet_3
			}
			add_energy = @human_fallen_empires_blackjack_bet_3
			add_energy = @human_fallen_empires_blackjack_bet_3
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = human_fallen_empires_blackjack_bet_4
			}
			add_energy = @human_fallen_empires_blackjack_bet_4
			add_energy = @human_fallen_empires_blackjack_bet_4
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = human_fallen_empires_blackjack_end_stay
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = human_fallen_empires_blackjack_bet_0
					}
					add_energy = @human_fallen_empires_blackjack_bet_0
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = human_fallen_empires_blackjack_bet_1
					}
					add_energy = @human_fallen_empires_blackjack_bet_1
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = human_fallen_empires_blackjack_bet_2
					}
					add_energy = @human_fallen_empires_blackjack_bet_2
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = human_fallen_empires_blackjack_bet_3
					}
					add_energy = @human_fallen_empires_blackjack_bet_3
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = human_fallen_empires_blackjack_bet_4
					}
					add_energy = @human_fallen_empires_blackjack_bet_4
				}
				else = {
					custom_tooltip = human_fallen_empires_blackjack_end_lose
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
